msg:Located in a busy part of the city, very close to Wulin Square and the grand canal, which is beautiful at night.  About 15 minute walk to the nearest metro, which was challenging in the heat.  I live in Shanghai, so getting around Hangzhou was fairly straightforward, with easy access to Metro and Didi services.  It is definitely worth a visit to the West Lake and Leifeng Temple; the view from the top is amazing.  The hotel staff were friendly on arrival and the standard of the room was better than expected for the price paid.  I didn't eat in the hotel or use the facilities much, so can't comment on those, but I have no complaints; checking in and out was straightforward and efficient, even with the Covid restrictions.  Overall, highly recommended and Hanzhou is an amazing city, well worth a visit.  Just check out my photos; picture 1 is a the view from my room on the 14th Floor.

When booking on Ctrip, I saw that Junting's score was higher than that of the conference hotel, and the reviews were full of praise. I finally chose Junting. Maybe the reviews I read made my expectations a bit high. Standing in the hotel, I didn't find many traces of design in the hotel's facilities. On the contrary, they looked a bit old and simple. There were no ironing tools, no sewing kit, and the small refrigerator was almost room temperature. Drawing the curtains across the sofa is a bit hard, and closing the small window requires some strength and skill. msg:Advantages: It is located on the roadside of the Wulin Business District Stadium, and is convenient for driving and subway. The hotel is new, the rooms are large, and the blue linens and bookshelves have an elegant feel. The reservation requires a high floor, so we arranged for the 14th floor. It is said that the executive room will be upgraded to the southwest corner, with floor-to-ceiling windows on two sides. It is spacious and bright, but there is no warm flush toilet seat in our room. The large writing table (which is rarely equipped in five-diamond hotels nowadays) is arranged overlapping with the couch (bed) and is movable. You can choose to face it from both sides. This design is great (but the movement is a bit too slippery). Service calls are centralized on the red ** button of the telephone, and services are arranged uniformly by the front desk. There are mobile service robots. Two bags of hanging ear coffee are provided in the room. The taste is slightly bitter but not sour, which is good. If you have milk, one bag can make two cups. There are not many varieties of breakfast but the quality is good.
Disadvantages: The lobby and restaurant are cramped like a fast hotel.
